## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / concentration-time dynamics)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is an ODE describing how concentration A changes with time t, which is the core object of chemical kinetics. With only A and t available, the most likely structures are empirical or mechanistic rate laws where dA_dt depends on A (reaction order, equilibrium relaxation, autocatalysis) and possibly an explicit time-dependent rate constant (temperature ramps, catalyst activation/deactivation, periodic forcing).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics (constant-rate process): dA_dt = c0 (e.g., constant feed/production or surface-limited consumption independent of A)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive/thermal decomposition, pseudo-first-order limit)
- General power-law (nth-order) kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical order; elementary step approximation when order is integer)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (net forward-backward balance giving approach to equilibrium concentration c1)
- Source-plus-sink (driven first-order): dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A (constant generation with proportional loss; sign of c1 sets decay vs growth)
- Shifted power-law (background/offset concentration): dA_dt = -c0 * (A + c1)**c2 (accounts for baseline, impurities, or variable substitution A' = A + c1)
- Autocatalytic / logistic-in-concentration form: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating kinetics with a limiting concentration scale c1)
- Generalized inhibition/retardation (nonlinear rational): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + A**c2) (rate slows at high A due to crowding, transport limits, or inhibitory effects)
- Time-ramped pseudo-first-order rate constant: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (temperature/programmed ramps or slowly changing environment)
- Catalyst deactivation/activation multiplier: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (effective rate constant changes exponentially with time)
- Stretched/exponentially modified time dependence: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t**c2) * A (nonlinear ramping, complex activation/deactivation kinetics)
- Periodic forcing (photochemical/flow modulation): dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (time-periodic illumination, feed, or mixing effects)
- Fractal/transport-limited effective kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (apparent rate constant varies as a power of time due to diffusion/aging of reactive sites)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope ŌåÆ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects ŌåÆ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay ŌåÆ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior ŌåÆ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects ŌåÆ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Reaction order fingerprint: if log(Abs(dA_dt)) vs log(A) is approximately linear over a range, the slope suggests a power-law order (use dA_dt ~ -c0 * A**c1).
- Equilibrium approach: if dA_dt crosses zero at a nonzero A and the dynamics settle there, include a steady-state term (A - c1) indicating reversible balance.
- Autocatalysis signature: if the magnitude of dA_dt is small at low A, increases to a peak at intermediate A, then decreases near a maximum A, use A*(c1-A).
- Background/measurement offset: if kinetics appear inconsistent near AŌēł0 (nonzero rate or curvature), try a shifted variable (A + c1) in the rate law.
- Time-varying environment: if the same A value produces different dA_dt at different times, include explicit k(t) factors such as (c0 + c1*t) or exp(c1*t).
- Induction period: if early-time rates are systematically suppressed relative to later times at similar A, model activation with an increasing k(t) multiplier on A-dependent terms.
- A-dependent slowing at high concentration: if rate increases with A at low values but plateaus/retards at high A, use a rational inhibition form A/(c1 + A**c2).
- Periodic perturbations: if dA_dt oscillates in time at fixed A (or residuals vs t are sinusoidal), modulate the rate constant with sin(c*t) or cos(c*t).

Final search results
============================================================
Best expression     : A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(A*c5)
Structure desc      : Additive mix of linear A, a power-law in A times a slowly decaying exponential in t, and an exponential in A. Since c1Ōēł1.086, the middle term is approximately proportional to A with coefficient c2*exp(c3 t) Ōēł ŌłÆ0.610*exp(ŌłÆ0.100 t), while the last term is a positive decaying exponential in A for A>0 (c4=0.945, c5=-0.528). Thus for moderate positive A the model behaves like an A-linear term with time-varying slope plus an offset-like exp(ŌłÆ0.528A); no coefficients are near zero, consistent with the extremely low NMSE.
Fitted params       : c0=-3.3096e-02, c1=1.0859e+00, c2=-6.1008e-01, c3=-1.0033e-01, c4=9.4517e-01, c5=-5.2799e-01
Train NMSE          : 1.78e-05
Test NMSE           : 1.78e-05
OOD Test NMSE       : 6.90e-03

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK7)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_w*cos(log(A + c3))
Candidate formulas: 194

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,A)= -0.7317701895\,A\,e^{-0.08162134037\,t}\;+\;0.840340505\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (by choosing its free constants) to produce **(i)** a term exactly of the form \(K\cdot A e^{\lambda t}\) with \(\lambda=-0.0816...\) and \(K=-0.73177...\), **plus** **(ii)** a term exactly of the form \(M\cos(\log(A+1))\) with \(M=0.84034...\). No other \(t\)-dependence or \(A\)-dependence can remain after parameter choices.

Below, I check each candidate for whether it even has the right *functional forms* available. If a candidate lacks either an \(A e^{\lambda t}\) term or a \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) term (or an exactly phase-shiftable equivalent), it cannot match.

---

### 1. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4*exp(A*c5)`
Has an \(A^{c1}e^{c3 t}\) term (can make \(c1=1\) to get \(A e^{c3 t}\)), but **no** \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) (only \(e^{A c5}\)). Cannot match.

### 2. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4/(A**c3 + c5)`
Has \(A e^{c2 t}\) possible, but the rational-in-\(A\) term cannot become \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.

### 3. `A*c0 + c1*exp(A*c2)*sin(c3 + c4*t) + c5*exp(c6*t)`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Also has \(e^{A c2}\) and sinusoid in \(t\), wrong structure. Cannot match.

### 4. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) and no \(A e^{\lambda t}\) (only \(e^{c4 t}\) without \(A\)). Cannot match.

### 5. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t)/(A + c4) + A*c5`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). The exponential term is \(A\exp(c3 t)/(A+c4)\), not \(A\exp(\lambda t)\) unless you force \((A+c4)\) constant, impossible. Cannot match.

### 6. `A**5*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**2*c2 + A*c3 + A*c4`
No cosine-log term; wrong powers. Cannot match.

### 7. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A**c3*c4*exp(c5*t)`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.

### 8. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2/(A**c1 + c3) + c4*exp(c5*t)`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.

### 9. `A*c0 + c1*log(c2*exp(A*c3) + 1) + c4*t/(c5*t + c6) + c7/(c5*t + c6)`
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\); also has rational-in-\(t\). Cannot match.

### 10. `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(A*c4 + c5*t) + 1) + c6) + c7*exp(A*c8)`
This has a sine of a log, but its log argument depends on both \(A\) and \(t\) unless \(c5=0\). If \(c5=0\), it becomes \(\sin(c2\log(c3|A c4|+1)+c6)\), which is \(\sin(\alpha\log(\beta|A|)+\dots)\), not \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) because inside is \(\log(\text{affine in }A)\) only if you can make \(c3|A c4|+1 = A+1\). With nonnegativity, \(|A c4|=A c4\) if \(c4\ge 0\). You could set \(c4=1,c3=1\) to get \(\log(A+1)\). Then sine can become cosine via phase shift: \(\sin(x+\pi/2)=\cos(x)\). So the cosine-log piece is achievable.
But the other required term \(-0.7317 A e^{-0.0816 t}\) is **not** present: the only \(t\)-dependence left (after setting \(c5=0\)) is none; there is no \(e^{\lambda t}\) multiplied by \(A\). The remaining \(A*c0\) is just linear in \(A\) with no \(e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 11. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2/(A**c1 + c3) + c4*t/(c5*t + c6) + c7/(c5*t + c6)`
No cosine-log; cannot match.

### 12. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t**c3) + c4*log(c5*exp(A*c6) + 1)`
Has \(A e^{c2 t^{c3}}\) (can set \(c3=1\) to get \(A e^{c2 t}\)), but second term is \(\log(1+c5 e^{A c6})\), not \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.

### 13. `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + c3*t/(c4*t + c5) + c6/(c4*t + c5)`
No cosine-log and wrong \(t\)-dependence. Cannot match.

### 14. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2*t + c3) + c4*exp(A*c5)*sin(c6 + c7*t) + c8/(c2*t + c3)`
No cosine-log; cannot match.

### 15. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2/(A**c1 + c3) + A**c4*c5*exp(c6*t)`
Has an \(A^{c4} e^{c6 t}\) term (can set \(c4=1\) for \(A e^{c6 t}\)), but no cosine-log. Cannot match.

### 16. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(...) + c9*sin(...)`
Sine-of-log type could be tuned to cosine-of-log, but there is no \(A e^{\lambda t}\) term at all. Cannot match.

### 17. `A*c0 + c1*exp(A*c2)*sin(c3 + c4*t) + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7`
No cosine-log; cannot match.

### 18. `c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(A*c4 + c5*t) + 1) + c6)`
Can produce cosine(log(A+1)) similarly by setting \(c5=0,c3=1,c4=1,c2=1\) and phase shift, but no \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 19. `A*c0 + A**c1*c2/(A**c1 + c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A*c7 + c8*t) + 1) + c9)`
Can get cosine(log(A+1)) by setting \(c8=0\) and tuning constants, but no \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 20. `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(c4*t) + 1) + c5)`
Log depends on \(t\) only; GT cosine depends on \(A\). Cannot match.

### 21. `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(A*c4 + c5*t) + 1) + c6) + c7*sin(c8*t + c9)`
Even if first sine-of-log is tuned to cosine(log(A+1)) by setting \(c5=0\), there is still no \(A e^{\lambda t}\) term; extra sine in \(t\) can be zeroed (set \(c7=0\)), but still missing exponential-decay term. Cannot match.

### 22. `A*c0 + A*c1*cos(c2*t + c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(...A...t...) + c9)`
Has cosine in \(t\) (not exponential), and sine-of-log could become cosine(log(A+1)) if \(t\) removed from inside by setting \(c8=0\). But the required \(A e^{-0.0816 t}\) cannot be made from \(A\cos(c2 t+c3)\). Cannot match.

### 23. `A*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)*Abs(A)**5`
No cosine-log; wrong \(A\) power. Cannot match.

### 24. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A + c2) + c3*sin(c4*log(...A...t...) + c8)`
Sine-of-log can be tuned to cosine(log(A+1)) by setting \(t\) coefficient to 0, but no \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 25. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*log(c4*exp(A*c5) + 1)`
Has \(A e^{c2 t}\) possible, but log-exp term cannot become cosine(log(A+1)). Cannot match.

### 26. `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(c4 + c5*t) + 1) + c6)`
Log depends on \(t\), not \(A\). Cannot match.

### 27. `A*c0 + A*c1/(c2*t + c3) + A**c4*c5/(A**c4 + c6) + c7/(c2*t + c3)`
No cosine-log and wrong \(t\)-dependence. Cannot match.

### 28. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*sin(c4*log(...A...t...) + c8)`
Could set \(c7=0\) inside Abs to remove \(t\) from log by setting the coefficient of \(t\) to 0; then sine-of-log can become cosine(log(A+1)). Good for the cosine-log part.
But the first term is \(A*c0\) plus \(A*c1 e^{c2 t}\). GT needs **only** \(-0.7317 A e^{-0.0816 t}\) (no additional plain \(A\) term). You could set \(c0=0\) and choose \(c1=-0.7317, c2=-0.0816\) to match the exponential term. Then choose sine parameters to match \(0.84034\cos(\log(A+1))\).  
However: the sine term is \(c3\sin(c4\log(c5|A c6|+1)+c8)\). To equal \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) for all \(A\), you need the inside to be exactly \(\log(A+1)\) (up to sign/scale that can be absorbed only if scale is 1; \(\cos(kx)\neq \cos(x)\) for all \(x\) unless \(k=\pm1\)). So set \(c4=1\), and make \(c5|A c6|+1 = A+1\) for all \(A\ge 0\): choose \(c6=1\), \(c5=1\) and use domain \(A\ge 0\) so \(|A|=A\). Then \(\sin(\log(A+1)+c8)\) becomes \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) by setting \(c8=\pi/2\) and amplitude \(c3=0.84034\).  
This seems structurally perfect **except** the candidateŌĆÖs log argument is `c5*Abs(A*c6 + c7*t) + 1` (from candidate 28: `Abs(A*c6 + c7*t)`), not `Abs(A*c6)` unless \(c7=0\). We can set \(c7=0\). Then it works.
So candidate 28 **can** match GT.

### 29. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t**c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(...A...t...) + c9)`
Same idea as 28; set \(c0=0\), \(c3=1\), \(c1=-0.73177\), \(c2=-0.0816213\). Set the sine-of-log part to cosine(log(A+1)) by setting \(t\) inside log to 0 and tuning as above. So candidate 29 can match as well.

### 30. `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2 + c3) + c4*exp(A*c5)*sin(c6 + c7*t) + c8/(A*c2 + c3)`
No cosine-log and has \(e^{A c5}\sin(\cdot t)\). Cannot match.

### 31. Big rational expression in \(A\) plus exp(t) terms
No cosine-log; also complicated rational dependence. Cannot match.

### 32. Same structure as 18 (sine of log of affine in A and t)
No \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 33. Adds `+ c7*log(A*c8 + 1)`
Still no \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 34. `A*c0 + A*c1 + sin(log(...)) + c8`
No \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 35. `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*Abs(A + c4*t) + 1) + c5)`
No \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 36. `A*c0 + A*c1 + c2*sin(c3 + c4*log(...))`
No \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 37. `A**5*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2 + c3*sin(log(...))`
Exponential term has \(A^5\), not \(A\). Cannot match.

### 38ŌĆō39. Variants with sine(log(...)) plus extra products
No \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 40. Logs of exp(A...) etc.
No cosine-log and no \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match.

### 41ŌĆō44. Include exp(A...) * sin(...) or exp(t) but no cosine(log(A+1)) except via sine-of-log in 44? (44 has sine-of-log but also exp(t))
44: has sine-of-log (can become cosine(log(A+1))) and has `+ c7*exp(c8*t)` but that exp(t) is not multiplied by \(A\). Missing \(A e^{\lambda t}\). Cannot match. Others lack cosine-log.

### 45. `A*c0 + c1*t**(1/3)` no.

### 46ŌĆō48, 52, 57ŌĆō63, 68, 71, 109, 116, 175, 178, 187, 193, 194
These are exp(A...)*sin(time) families; none can produce \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) and also the needed \(A e^{\lambda t}\) simultaneously. Cannot match.

### 49ŌĆō51, 53ŌĆō56, 64ŌĆō67, 69ŌĆō70, 72ŌĆō75, 77ŌĆō83, 84ŌĆō99, 101ŌĆō108, 110ŌĆō174, 176ŌĆō192
All of these lack at least one of the two required distinctive structures:
- either they have no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) / sine-of-log-in-\(A\) term at all, **or**
- they have sine-of-log but no \(A e^{\lambda t}\) term (only linear \(A\), rational in \(t\), polynomials, etc.), **or**
- they have \(A e^{\lambda t}\) but the other term is log/exp/rational rather than cosine(log(A+1)).

Given GTŌĆÖs very specific combination (exponential in \(t\) times \(A\), plus cosine of log of affine in \(A\)), the only candidates that contain **both** an \(A\cdot \exp(\text{const}\cdot t)\) term and a sine-of-log-in-\(A\) term that can be phase-shifted into cosine are **28 and 29**.

## Explicit matching parameter choice (example for candidate 28)
Candidate 28:
\[
A c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + c3\sin\!\big(c4\log(c5|A c6 + c7 t|+1)+c8\big).
\]
Choose (domain \(A\ge 0\)):
- \(c0=0\)
- \(c1=-0.731770189531933\)
- \(c2=-0.0816213403667534\)
- \(c7=0\) (remove \(t\) from the log argument)
- \(c6=1,\;c5=1\) so \(|A|=A\) and log argument is \(A+1\)
- \(c4=1\)
- \(c8=\pi/2\) so \(\sin(\log(A+1)+\pi/2)=\cos(\log(A+1))\)
- \(c3=0.840340504979681\)

Then candidate 28 becomes exactly the GT.

Same style works for candidate 29 with \(t^{c3}\) forced to \(t\) by \(c3=1\).

**GT:** `-0.731770189531933*A*exp(-0.0816213403667534*t) + 0.840340504979681*cos(log(A + 1))`

This has two terms:
1. A term proportional to `A*exp(-╬▒t)` (exponential decay in t, linear in A)
2. A term `cos(log(A+1))` (depends only on A, not t)

Let me analyze the key structural features:
- The first term couples A and t through `A*exp(ct)`
- The second term is `cos(log(A+1))` which depends only on A

**Key observations for filtering:**
- Need a term like `A*exp(c*t)` (or equivalent time-dependent coupling with A)
- Need a term like `cos(log(A+1))` - this is a very specific function of A only

- `cos(log(A+1))` directly
- `sin(log(A+1) + ŽĆ/2)` = `cos(log(A+1))`
- Note: `log(A+1)` when AŌēź0 ranges from 0 to Ōł×

- `A^c1*c2/(A^c1 + c3)` - this is `c2/(1 + c3*A^(-c1))`, a sigmoid-like function, NOT `cos(log(A+1))`
- `log(c*exp(Ac) + 1)` - this is a softplus, NOT `cos(log(A+1))`
- `sin(c*log(c*|A*c + c*t| + 1) + c)` - this could potentially work if we can set the t-coefficient to 0

Now I also need `A*exp(c*t)` for the first term.
